<!-- Content Header -->
<header class="content-header grid__10-article">
	<h1 class="content-header__headline">Martellus Bennett responds to critics, asks if they would be willing to take a pay cut</h1>
	<h2 class="content-header__subheadline">&quot;And stop @&#039;ing me about taking less money.&quot;</h2>
</header><!-- /content-header -->
				
<div class="grid__8-centered">
	<figure class="content-media content-media--inline-center">

		<div class="wrapper lead-media" data-og-width="640">

			<img srcset="https://www.boston.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/02/martellusandgronk-850x478$large.jpeg 850w, https://www.boston.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/02/martellusandgronk-850x478$medium.jpeg 640w, https://www.boston.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/02/martellusandgronk-850x478$small.jpeg 330w, https://www.boston.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/02/martellusandgronk-850x478$xsmall.jpeg 240w" sizes="(min-width:850px) 850px, (min-width:330px) 640px, 330px" class="content-media__image" alt="BOSTON, MA - FEBRUARY 07: Rob Gronkowski and Martellus Bennett of the New England Patriots celebrate during the Super Bowl victory parade on February 7, 2017 in Boston, Massachusetts. The Patriots defeated the Atlanta Falcons 34-28 in overtime in Super Bowl 51. (Photo by Billie Weiss/Getty Images)" />			<figcaption class="content-media__caption">
				Rob Gronkowski and Martellus Bennett celebrate during the Patriots&#039; Super Bowl victory parade earlier this month.				<span class="content-media__credit">
					–Billie Weiss / Getty Images				</span>
			</figcaption>

		</div>

	</figure>
</div>
				
<!-- Content Byline -->
<div class="content-byline">
			<div class="content-byline__commentary">By</div>
				<div class="content-byline__producer">
			<a href="https://www.boston.com/author/n-decosta-klipa" title="Posts by Nik DeCosta-Klipa" class="author url fn" rel="author">Nik DeCosta-Klipa</a>		</div>
			<div class="content-byline__timestamp">February 22, 2017</div>
</div><!-- /content-byline -->
				
	<div class="content-newsletter-cta">
		<p>Get Patriots game stats and the inside scoop on the season with <a href="http://pages.email.bostonglobe.com/BDC_PointAfterSignUp/">The Boston Globe's Point After newsletter</a> delivered for free to your inbox.</p>
	</div>

				
<!-- Content Text -->
<div class="content-text content-text-article">
	<p>Following <a href="https://www.boston.com/sports/new-england-patriots/2017/02/22/morning-sports-update-martellus-bennett-leaving-the-patriots-is-a-real-possibility" target="_blank">reports</a> he might leave the New England Patriots, tight end Martellus Bennett turned the question around on those asking him to stay for less money: Would they take a pay cut at their jobs?</p>
<blockquote class="twitter-tweet" data-width="500">
<p lang="en" dir="ltr">And stop @'ing me about taking less money. You take less money and your job? All of you take a pay cut hahaha.</p>
<p>— Martellus Bennett (@MartysaurusRex) <a href="https://twitter.com/MartysaurusRex/status/834521286814613504">February 22, 2017</a></p></blockquote>
<p><script async src="//platform.twitter.com/widgets.js" charset="utf-8"></script></p>
<p>Bennett also characterized the reporting on his impending free agency decision as “<a href="https://twitter.com/MartysaurusRex/status/834520421873639436" target="_blank">irresponsible</a>” <a href="https://twitter.com/MartysaurusRex/status/834520683367522312" target="_blank">speculation</a> and dismissed a Twitter user’s accusation that he was basking in the attention.</p>
<blockquote class="twitter-tweet" data-width="500">
<p lang="en" dir="ltr">Bro I don't care about this attention shit. What does having your attention do to better my life? You have no idea what you're talking about <a href="https://t.co/WPVjwf5FJs">https://t.co/WPVjwf5FJs</a></p>
<p>— Martellus Bennett (@MartysaurusRex) <a href="https://twitter.com/MartysaurusRex/status/834522350573985793">February 22, 2017</a></p></blockquote>
<p><script async src="//platform.twitter.com/widgets.js" charset="utf-8"></script></p>
<p>“All I’m saying is cut your own grass don’t be all in my garden f[—]ing with my fruit while weeds are growing all over yours,” he <a href="https://twitter.com/MartysaurusRex/status/834523343944634369" target="_blank">vented</a>, before ending the series of tweets on a note of well wishes.</p>
<blockquote class="twitter-tweet" data-width="500">
<p lang="en" dir="ltr">Anyways I love you all. 🤗🤗 I hope you all get a raise today or tomorrow.</p>
<p>— Martellus Bennett (@MartysaurusRex) <a href="https://twitter.com/MartysaurusRex/status/834523570227335168">February 22, 2017</a></p></blockquote>
<div class="ad-container ad-container--supelead1">
			<span class="ad-container__notification-text">Advertisement</span>
		<div class="ad-container__notification">
		<div class="ad-container__ad-slot">
					<div id="div-gpt-ad-supelead1" class="dfp-ad dfp-supelead1" data-ad-unit="supelead1"></div>
			</div>
			</div>
	</div><p><script async src="//platform.twitter.com/widgets.js" charset="utf-8"></script></p>
<p>After <a href="http://archive.boston.com/sports/football/patriots/2016/03/16/patriots-reportedly-trading-for-tight-end-martellus-bennett/kKCVhDvU5CiX2CPxgMgiwI/story.html" target="_blank">being traded to the Patriots</a> in the final year of his contract last year, Bennett made 55 receptions for 701 yards and seven touchdowns during the 2016 regular season. With fellow tight end Rob Gronkowski sidelined due to injury, the newcomer also played a key role in the team’s Super Bowl run.</p>
<p>NFL.com’s Ian Rapoport <a href="http://www.nfl.com/news/story/0ap3000000787107/article/martellus-bennett-will-test-freeagent-market" target="_blank">reported</a> Tuesday that it was a “real possibility” that Bennett leaves the Patriots this offseason, as the team is unwilling to pay him a salary over Gronkowski’s $9 million annual figure. Bennett <a href="https://twitter.com/BenVolin/status/710247016874508289" target="_blank">reportedly</a> made just over $5 million this past season.</p></div> <!-- /content-text -->
